I haven't recovered from jet leg.
I'm out like a light.
go out like a light　
英 美
(美俚)醉得不省人事, 被打昏, 昏睡

今日短语
在英语中，go out 是一个被用来形容火、光、热“熄灭”的短语。成语 go out like a light 其实就是通过光亮熄灭的速度很快这一特征，来比喻某人“立马就入睡、瞬间就失去意识”，它的第一种含义类似于汉语里所说的“一沾枕头就能睡着”。

例句
I have no problem sleeping, I go out like a light as soon as I hit the pillow.
我睡眠一向很好，只要一沾枕头，马上就能睡着。

My daughter seems to love this lullaby. She goes out like a light when I hum it to her.
看来我女儿很喜欢这首摇篮曲。每当我哼唱这段旋律时她就会立刻睡着。

I'm not sure if I should lay down in bed right after dinner – I'd probably go out like a light.
我不知道是不是该吃完晚饭后就立刻躺下，我很可能一沾枕头就睡着了。

2021-4-1
tricky　扩展词汇　
英 ['trɪki] 　 　 美 ['trɪki] 　 　
adj. 棘手的；狡猾的；巧妙的

Singluar subjects take a singular verb.
My dog wats dinner.
Non-count subjects take a singular verb.
Plural subjects take a plural verb.
The books are all over the floor.

gerund　畅通词汇　
英 ['dʒerənd] 　 　 美 ['dʒerənd] 　 　
n. 动名词

Gerunds take a singular verb.
Singing is my favourite hobby.

Irregykar okyrak subjects take a plural verb.
People talk to me on the bus every day.
The police are coming to stop the robbery.


Nouns joined by "and" take a plural verb.
Maria and Antonio have a baby.
Snow and ice make driving dangerous.

When the subject includes a prepositional phrase,the noun that comes before the position agrees with the verb.
One of the leaders was guilty.
Members of that group are organizing a fundraiser.

fundraiser　
英 ['fʌndˌreɪzə] 　 　 美 ['fʌndˌreɪzə] 　 　
n. 资金筹集人；资金筹集活动

Each and every take a singular verb.
Each component is sold sepaarately.
Every reporter wants to do that interview.

2.The pronouns everyboday/everone and nobody/no one take a singular verb.
Everyone was tired.

3.Non-count nouns that end in -s take a singular verb.
Her good news was a relief.
Mathematics is my firs class of the day.


4.Subjects about time,money,or distance take a singular verb.
Five hours is enough sleep for me.
One thousand dollars was my gift to him.

5.Collective nouns(family team,staff,etc) usually take a singular verb,especially in American and Canadian English。
My family has three dos and a cat.
Our team wins the competition every year.

6.When the subject includes certain quantifiers(all,a lot,most,some,none,etc.) and a repositional phrase,the verb agrees with the noun after the preposition.
A lot of my friends have therir own cars.
A lot of rain is in the forecast.

7.When the subject includes a fraction or a percentage,the verb agrees with the nuoun after the preposition.
Half of the pasta is vegetarian.
Only 25% of the survey results were favourable.

8.The subject "a number of "+ noun takes a plural verb, while "the number of "+ noun takes a singular verb.
A number of articles deal with this topic.
The number of attacks is increasing.

英语中有16种时态
1.一般现在时 the present tense
2.一般过去时 the past tense
3.一般将来时 the future tense
4.一般过去将来时 the past future tense
5.现在进行时 the present continuous tense
6.过去进行时 the past Continuous Tense
7.将来进行时 the future continuous tense
8.过去将来进行时 the past future continuous tense
9.现在完成时 the Present Perfect Tense
10.过去完成时 the Past Perfect Tense
11.将来完成时 the future perfect tense
12.过去将来完成时 the past future perfect tense
13.现在完成进行时 the present perfect continuous tense
14.过去完成进行时 the past perfect continuous tense
15.将来完成进行时 the future perfect continuous tense
16.过去将来完成进行时 the past future perfect continuous tense

Infinitives　
英 美
n. 不定式（infinitive的复数）；原形动词

Infinitives are common after an adjective.
It's nice to meet you.
It was dangerous to stand near that machine.

Infinitives can follow a noun or pronoun.
You ask me to call you.
The doctor advised Mark to eat more vegetables.

ask choose decide get need plan promise want
They want to get their test back as soon as possible
The sudents are planing to have a party this friday.


Could I bring one by later?
It was touch-and-go whether we would get to the airport in time.

2021-12-05
It's the thought that counts 
是一句礼貌用语，通常用在赠送礼物的场景中。 
尽管收礼人可能不喜欢收到的礼物，但仍想感谢送礼人的一片心意的时候，就可以说
It's the thought that counts.”，也就是我们说的“心意最重要，礼轻情意重”。

token　常用词汇　
英 ['təʊkən] 　 　 美 ['toʊkən] 　 　
n. 象征；标志；纪念品；代币；代价券；[语言学]语言符号
adj. 象征性的；装样子的

token of my appreciation       
在中文中翻译"token of my appreciation"
表示我的感谢为了感谢你一点心意聊表谢意 
I wanted to give you this as a token of my appreciation.
我想给你这个表示我的感谢.

Get in someone’s hair
得到某人的頭髮?  這是什麼奇怪的意思啊? 千萬別誤會，其實 get in someone’s hair，就是說正在打擾或惹惱別人。
例如：Susan was trying to prepare dinner, but her children were getting in her hair! 
這句話的意思是說當蘇珊做飯時，她的孩子們在打擾她。
如果有人正在煩你，你就可以說：Get out of my hair!

freeloader　
英 ['friːləʊdə(r)] 　 　 美 ['friːloʊdər] 　 　
n. 不速之客；吃白食的人

Detective:

Thanks for offering to show me the crime scene, Lila. Can you tell me where you were the night the ring disappeared? 

Lila:

I was out buying a birthday gift for my husband. It's under Cynthia's bed if you don't believe me. I know from your show you like to see things for yourself.

Detective:

That won't be necessary. Tell me about your marriage.

Lila:

I can't complain. We're still together, aren't we? 

Detective:

Let me put this a different way. Does Ralph treat you well?

Lila:

He doesn't exactly go the extra mile. I wouldn't mind a token of appreciation from time to time.

Detective:

Do you wish he was more like…Paul?

Lila:

Are you kidding? All Paul does is gawk at Emma. I wish Ralph was more like my father. A day never went by when he didn't treat my mother to something special.

Detective:

Do you mean like…jewelry?

Lila:

Money can't buy you love, Detective. It's the thought that counts. My father put a lot of thought into his gifts. They didn't always come in a pretty box.

Detective:

What's the best gift your father ever gave your mother?

Lila:

A day off from the kids! I could still use a hand with the twins even though they're fully grown.

Detective:

You mean you wish Ralph would pay more attention to the twins?

Lila:

Emma could use a different shoulder to cry on once in a while. She's not always a happy camper.

Detective:

What about Oliver? He needs someone to talk to man-to-man, doesn't he?

Lila:

You took the words out of my mouth, Detective. I'm worried Oliver is going to be a freeloader forever.

Detective:

It sounds to me like you want your son out of your hair.

Back up
Reverse; move a vehicle backwards
He backed up close to the gate.

Break down
Stop working.
The car broke down on the way home.

Change /shift up
Start using a higher gear.
When he got on the motorway he was able to change up to fifth (gear).

Change /gear/shift/down
Start using a lower gear.
I changed down from fourth to third as we approached the town.

Cut in
Cut off
Suddenly move very closely in front of another vehicle in a dangerous manner.
That car just cut in/cut me off and I almost hit it!

Drive off
Leave a place in a vehicle.
The bank robber drove off in a black car.

Drive on
Continue driving.
That’s my boss. Don’t stop –drive on! I don't want him to see me.

Drop off
Take someone somewhere (by car).
Jack dropped me off at the station.
Fill up
Put fuel in the tank.
I’ll stop at a petrol station and fill up.
Knock down
Hit someone with a vehicle.
A cyclist was knocked down by a truck.
Pick up
Go somewhere in your car and collect someone
John offered to pick up his colleague at the bus stop.

Pull in
Move to a designated place at the side of the road.
A police car signalled to me to pull in.

Pull off
Leave the road momentarily.
I was tired from driving so I pulled off for a rest and a cup of coffee.
Pull out
Move out from the roadside onto the road.
A motorbike suddenly pulled out in front of me.
Pull over
Move over to the side of the road.
She pulled over to make way for the ambulance.
Pull up
Stop.
All vehicles must pull up at the traffic lights.
Slow down
Reduce the speed
The driver slowed down in front of the school.
Speed up
Accelerate
I’ll have to speed up if we want to arrive on time.
Turn off
Leave a road to take another.
Is this where we turn off?

2022-6-2
表示将来某一时间正在进行的动作，一般带状语。When he comes to my house tomorrow， I will be writing the report.
表示现在正在进行的动作，但这个动作会延续到将来。I think that she will be working on this experiment until next morning.
表示预定的将来动作或对将来的预测，并非人为安排.After you take the medicine， you will be feeling much better.
表示委婉的请求When shall we be meeting again?
表示原因Please come tomorrow afternoon，I'll be having a meeting tomorrow morning.
表示结果Stop the child or he will be falling over.
表示对将来的打算（区别于对将来的预测）My duties will be ending in July ， and I'll be returning to ShangHai.

她的工作总是很有条理。

她在一封长信里阐明了辞职原因。

她把国际象棋的棋子摆在棋盘上了。
We set out with enough provisions.
我们带上足够的食品出发了。

他欣然同意，我们就出发了。
They set out on the last stage of their journey.
他们开始了旅行的最后一程。
